bbw.chat.mode.vertical=模式：垂直 - 从原方块向上和向下延伸。顶面/底面无建筑物
bbw.chat.mode.nolock=模式：无锁定 - 从原方块向左、向右、向上和向下扩展。

lotr.waypoint.KUNZEKDUM=Kunzek-dûm
lotr.waypoint.KUNZEKDUM.info=Kunzek-dûm, the home city of the Stonefoot clan in the far south of the Red Mountains. Kunzek-dûm was not known for it wealth in gold or gems, but for its magnificent beauty. The city has never been sacked or sieged, for it is in the far south where few other people live even orcs. It is said that the city was built in a massive cave, and that the dwarves did not delve it so much as enhance the natural beauty of the city, carving great pillars into the stone, and polishing the crystals through out the cave so that it sparkles everywhere as if a thousand lamps were lit all about. They carved great designs into the stone walls, and built canals to each of the many great lakes through out the cavern. Thus Kunzek-dûm was known for its great beauty, and was marveled at by all other dwarves of Arda.
lotr.waypoint.KHAZADGOND=Khazad-Gônd
lotr.waypoint.KHAZADGOND.info=Khazad-Gônd, the home city of the Blacklock clan in the far north of the Red Mountains. Khazad-Gônd main riches was neither trade, gold or silver, even though they had plenty of the latter two. But it was in gems in forms of diamonds, rubies sapphires and opals. Which brought them great wealth and well decorated halls. The valley below the city was nicknamed "Valley of Coal" As in its early days the valley was extremely rich in ore veins of coal and logs, which was turned into charcoal for early forging.
